<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовый</a> (2234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сса</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mássa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mássovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mass, bulk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:убийство.html>уби́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mássovoje</b> ubíjstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mass</b> murder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mass; <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:массовый.html>ма́ссовая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mássovaja</b> kulʹtúra</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mass</b> culture, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a></b> culture</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мастеръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">masterŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Master of the Order</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">maistre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">magister</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">master, chief, head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мэтр.html>мэтр</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mɛtr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>

***масштаб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:масштаб.html>масшта́б</a> (3045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Maßstab</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масштаб.html>масшта́б</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">masštáb</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масштаб.html>масшта́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масштаб.html>масшта́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масштаб.html>масшта́бов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scale (ratio of distances)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scope</li>
<li>caliber</li>
<li>repute</li>
<li>standard</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:масштаб.html>масшта́б</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">masštáb</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scale <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dimension</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a> (5185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Russian Wikipedia has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%BC%D0%B0%D1%82_(%D1%88%D0%B0%D1%85%D0%BC%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%8B)" class="extiw" title="w:ru:мат (шахматы)"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:шахматы.html>ша́хматы</a>)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%BC%D0%B0%D1%82_(%D1%88%D0%B0%D1%85%D0%BC%D0%B0%D1%82%D1%8B)" class="extiw" title="w:ru:мат (шахматы)">Wikipedia <sup>ru</sup></a></span></div>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></i>, short for <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">échec et <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">شَاهُ مَاتَ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šāhu māta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">شاه مات</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šâh mât</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the king is amazed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́тов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chess</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> checkmate, mate (Russian notation: ×)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mattus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́та</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(singular only)</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a>, matte finish, frost <i>(glass)</i></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́та</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foul language; language that includes obscene words deriving from a small set of roots for sex, sexual organs, and sexuality
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрывать.html>покрыва́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́том</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pokryvátʹ <b>mátom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to heap scurrilous abuse on someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:благой.html>благи́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́том</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kričátʹ blagím <b>mátom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scream blue murder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***материал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a> (1072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">materialis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">material</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">materiál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>material, stuff
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">термоизоляцио́нный <a href = vnd.unilang:строительный.html>строи́тельный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">termoizoljaciónnyj stroítelʹnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">thermo-insulating building materials</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">чистосо́ртный <a href = vnd.unilang:лесной.html>лесно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čistosórtnyj lesnój <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">clean timber</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отснять.html>отсня́тый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otsnjátyj <b>materiál</b> fílʹma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">footage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:справочный.html>спра́вочный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">správočnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">reference source</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">абрази́вный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">abrazívnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">abradant, abrasive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">лесопоса́дочный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lesoposádočnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">saplings</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подручный.html>подру́чный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podrúčnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">improvised material; material at hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">шлифова́льный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šlifoválʹnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">abradant, abrasive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следственный.html>сле́дственный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slédstvennyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">evidence</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сопротивление.html>сопротивле́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лов</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soprotivlénije <b>materiálov</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">strength of materials, resistance of materials</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">упако́вочный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">upakóvočnyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">packaging material</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фактический.html>факти́ческий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">faktíčeskij <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the facts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́лах</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ekonómitʹ na <b>materiálax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to save on materials</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опубликовать.html>опублико́ванный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">opublikóvannyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">release</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fabric, material
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:материал.html>материа́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélyj <b>materiál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">white</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***материть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:материть.html>матери́ть</a> (23111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материть.html>матери́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">materítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обматери́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dirty mouth, to badmouth, to abuse, to cuss out <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to insult, to swear dirtily (at)</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:материя.html>мате́рия</a> (4213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">materia</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материя.html>мате́рия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">matérija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материя.html>мате́рии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материя.html>мате́рии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:материя.html>мате́рий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>substance, matter</li>
<li>fabric, material, cloth</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вещество.html>вещество́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">veščestvó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:субстанция.html>субста́нция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">substáncija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:матерный.html>ма́терный</a> (14389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ма́тер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">máter-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based off of the oblique stem of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">matʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">obscene language</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from the same word.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерный.html>ма́терный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">máternyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obscene, bad, dirty, foul</li></ol>

***матерщина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>матерщина</a> (21833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>матерщи́на</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́терщина</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">materščína</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">máterščina</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерщина.html>матерщи́ны</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерщина.html>ма́терщины</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерщина.html>матерщи́ны</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерщина.html>ма́терщины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерщина.html>матерщи́н</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матерщина.html>ма́терщин</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foul language, filthy language</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Occasionally some speakers stress the first syllable: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>ма́терщина</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">máterščina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or pronounce the word either as <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">матерши́на</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">materšína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ма́тершина</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">máteršina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">матерши́на</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">materšína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>common misspelling</i>)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нецензу́рщина</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">necenzúrščina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>the unquotable, unprintable, word(s) or expression(s)</i>)</li></ul>
